<li id='2024-10-05'><ul class='climbing-entry-header'><li><strong>5. 10. 2024</strong> (at <a href='https://www.boulderhaus.net/boulderhaus-heidelberg/'><img class='climbing-wall-logo' src='/climbing/wall-logos/boulderhaus.svg' alt='Logo of the Boulderhaus climbing wall.'/></a>)</li> <li><mark class='climbing-diary-record climbing-red climbing-red-text'><strong><span class='underline'>1</span></strong> [<a class='climbing-link' href='/climbing/videos/boulderhaus-red-2024-10-05-kfqqrxdd.mp4'>A</a>]</mark> </li></ul><p class='climbing-note'>Better.</p></li>

<li id='2024-10-04'><ul class='climbing-entry-header'><li><strong>4. 10. 2024</strong> (at <a href='https://www.boulderhaus.net/boulderhaus-heidelberg/'><img class='climbing-wall-logo' src='/climbing/wall-logos/boulderhaus.svg' alt='Logo of the Boulderhaus climbing wall.'/></a>)</li> </ul><p class='climbing-note'>Worst session in months. This note will be a bit longer.</p><p class='climbing-note'>First off, I managed to somehow <strong>pull a muscle while warming up</strong> (and by warming up I mean climbing a few 'easier' routes), which is really fucking stupid and should not happen. <strong>I need to warm up better</strong> to prevent things like this from happening.</p><p class='climbing-note'>Second (but kind of tied to first), the warm up was <strong>nowhere long enough</strong> to get properly warm before trying the routes, resulting in really bad first attempts on harder routes that went completely to waste.</p><p class='climbing-note'>Third, the attempts on the hard routes were done <strong>without breaks in between,</strong> which I often do, but not to this extent ‚Äì throwing yourself at a route does not help and is, again, <strong>fucking stupid.</strong></p><p class='climbing-note'>These three things resulted in a completely wasted session.</p><p class='climbing-note'>From now on, things will change. No warmup blues. No 5 seconds of brushing between ground attempts. I will, instead, be doing the following:</p><p class='climbing-note'><ul><li class='climbing-note'><strong>At least 15 minutes of warm-up</strong> ‚Äì maybe not ideal, but a start.</li><li class='climbing-note'><strong>At least 3 minute break between attempts</strong>, which is around 100x more than now.</li></ul></p><p class='climbing-note'>If not, I will find you Tom. I know where you live.</p></li>

<li id='2024-10-02'><ul class='climbing-entry-header'><li><strong>2. 10. 2024</strong> (at <a href='https://www.boulderhaus.net/boulderhaus-heidelberg/'><img class='climbing-wall-logo' src='/climbing/wall-logos/boulderhaus.svg' alt='Logo of the Boulderhaus climbing wall.'/></a>)</li> <li><mark class='climbing-diary-record climbing-red climbing-red-text'><strong><span class='underline'>3</span></strong></mark> </li></ul><p class='climbing-note'>The new routes are h.a.r.d.</p></li>

At least I finished the blue one I made progress on yesterday and tried a few new yellow ones to do.</p></li>

<li id='2021-08-13'><ul class='climbing-entry-header'><li><strong>13. 8. 2021</strong> (at <a href='https://www.lezeckecentrum.cz/cs/'><img class='climbing-wall-logo' src='/climbing/wall-logos/smichoff.svg' alt='Logo of the Sm√≠choff climbing wall.'/></a>)</li> <li><mark class='climbing-diary-record climbing-blue climbing-blue-text'><strong><span class='underline'>3</span></strong> [<a class='climbing-link' href='/climbing/videos/smichoff-blue-2021-08-13-igugpzvf.mp4'>A</a><a class='climbing-link' href='/climbing/videos/smichoff-blue-2021-08-13-ospctkyx.mp4'>A</a><a class='climbing-link' href='/climbing/videos/smichoff-blue-2021-08-13-qfmbmgtd.mp4'>A</a>]</mark> <mark class='climbing-diary-record climbing-yellow climbing-yellow-text'><strong><span class='underline'>1</span></strong> [<a class='climbing-link' href='/climbing/videos/smichoff-yellow-2021-08-13-xhqnbtjp.mp4'>A</a>]</mark> </li></ul><p class='climbing-note'>Today's gravity felt pretty good!</p></li>
